***допинг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:допинг.html>до́пинг</a> (25259)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">doping</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допинг.html>до́пинг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dóping</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допинг.html>до́пинга</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допинг.html>до́пинги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допинг.html>до́пингов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stimulant, performance-enhancing drug, dope <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">any illicit drug</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:официальный.html>официа́льный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:допинг.html>до́пинг</a></b>-контро́ль <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:осуществлённый.html>осуществлён</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:олимпийский.html>олимпи́йских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игр</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> грено́бле.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pérvyj oficiálʹnyj <b>dóping</b>-kontrólʹ byl osuščestvljón vo vrémja Olimpíjskix igr v Grenóble.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The first official <b>dope</b> control was carried out during the Olympic Games in Grenoble.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дописать.html>допи́сать</a> (17811)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дописать.html>дописа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dopisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дописывать.html>допи́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to finish <i>(writing)</i></li>
<li>to write <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to write in addition, to add</li>
<li>to finish <i>(painting)</i>, to paint in addition</li></ol>

***дописываемый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дописываемый.html>допи́сываемый</a> (26564)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дописываемый.html>допи́сываемый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dopísyvajemyj</span>)
</p>

***доползший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доползший.html>допо́лзший</a> (16732)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доползший.html>допо́лзший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dopólzšij</span>)
</p>

***дополнительно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дополнительный.html>дополни́тельно</a> (10612)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дополнительный.html>дополни́тельный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dopolnítelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дополнительный.html>дополни́тельно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dopolnítelʹno</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дополнять.html>дополня́ть</a> (13784)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дополнить.html>допо́лнить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dopólnitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дополнять.html>дополня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dopolnjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дополнить.html>допо́лнить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to supplement, to add, to amplify, to supply, to enlarge, to expand, to complete, to fill up</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:допрашивающий.html>допра́шивающий</a> (7191)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***допускать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:допускать.html>допуска́ть</a> (3819)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допускать.html>допуска́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dopuskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допустить.html>допусти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to admit</li>
<li>to accept, to permit, to allow, to tolerate</li>
<li>to assume
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:допускать.html>допуска́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́сли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne <b>dopuskájet</b> étoj mýsli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it doesn't occur to him</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:допускать.html>допуска́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étovo nelʹzjá <b>dopuskátʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this cannot be tolerated</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:допустить.html>допусти́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́менам</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó ne dopustíli k ekzámenam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was not admitted to the test</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допуск.html>до́пуск</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dópusk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:допустимый.html>допусти́мый</a> (2531)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допустимый.html>допусти́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dopustímyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>permissible, acceptable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:допустимый.html>допусти́мое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:произношение.html>произноше́ние</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dopustímoje</b> proiznošénije</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">acceptable pronunciation (in dictionaries)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>justifiable</li></ol>
